  [1mRoot Cause Analysis[22m

  The [38;2;177;185;249mdemo-buggy[39m program crashes with a [1mNULL pointer dereference[22m
  ([38;2;177;185;249mEXC_BAD_ACCESS[39m) in the [38;2;177;185;249madd_score[39m function at line 26.

  [2mCrash Details:[22m

  - [1mLocation[22m: [38;2;177;185;249mdemo-buggy.c:26[39m in [38;2;177;185;249madd_score()[39m function
  - [1mError[22m: [38;2;177;185;249mEXC_BAD_ACCESS (code=1, address=0x0)[39m
  - [1mInstruction[22m: [38;2;177;185;249ms->scores[s->num_scores] = score;[39m

  [2mRoot Cause:[22m

  The [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m field in the Student structure is [1mnever allocated memory[22m. When
   the program attempts to add a score to Alice:

  1. The Student struct is created with [38;2;177;185;249mscores = NULL[39m (0x0000000000000000)
  2. [38;2;177;185;249madd_score(alice, 95.5)[39m is called from [38;2;177;185;249mmain:56[39m
  3. The function tries to access [38;2;177;185;249ms->scores[0][39m which dereferences a NULL
  pointer
  4. This causes an immediate segmentation fault

  [2mVariables at Crash:[22m

  - [38;2;177;185;249ms[39m (Student pointer): Valid pointer [38;2;177;185;249m0x0000000140605580[39m

  - [38;2;177;185;249ms->age[39m: 20
  - [38;2;177;185;249ms->scores[39m: [1mNULL[22m ([38;2;177;185;249m0x0000000000000000[39m) â† [1mThis is the problem[22m
  - [38;2;177;185;249ms->num_scores[39m: 0
  - [38;2;177;185;249mscore[39m: 95.5

  The program needs to allocate memory for the [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m array before
  attempting to store values in it.
